# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="8f305-102">Membres obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8f305-103">Les tableaux de cet article listent les membres de type obsolètes dans le .NET Framework 4.5 et versions ultérieures, organisés par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8f305-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des membres obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8f305-105">Cet article ne liste pas les membres des types obsolètes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8f305-106">Pour obtenir la liste des types obsolètes, consultez [Types obsolètes](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="8f305-141">Les tableaux suivants répertorient les membres obsolètes dans les assemblys système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8f305-142">Ces assemblys sont utilisés pour le développement d’applications à usage général qui ciblent le .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8f305-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
